name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Family Tent - with View (2 beds)

posted:Posted February 16, 2024
msg:Overall, I was very satisfied. We played the front mountain on the first day and arrived at the entrance at about 12 noon. We basically went to all the projects in the front mountain, and then went to the back mountain to ski in the late afternoon. We saw wild monkeys on the way and arrived at the hotel at about 6:30 in the evening. The hotel staff helped us take our bags after we went up the first cable car and put them at the cable car to the back mountain. We played the front mountain lightly, which was very relaxing and not tiring. There were also staff to pick us up at the back mountain. The overall connection was good and there was no waste of time. On the second day, there were also staff to drive us back, so it was quite easy all the way.
The best scenery in the lower area should be Building 11 where we lived. The view is very good, not worse than the upper area, and it is the closest to the front desk and the place to eat breakfast and lunch, and it also feels the safest. The effect of the heating and electric blanket in the room is so good. If you cover the quilt at night, you don‚Äôt need to turn on the heating. It‚Äôs very warm.
The next day, before we checked out, we put our luggage in the room and went to the nearby Yunzhong Farm, which was only a hundred meters away from the hotel. The children picked up 5 pheasant eggs, caught a crucian carp with their bare hands, and boiled pheasant eggs in the hot spring pool. They were delicious.
Let me talk about two slightly lacking places. One is that the bathroom should be enclosed like a shower room, and the other is that the wind is very strong after sleeping at night, blowing the tent to move, as if there are small animals crawling on it, especially in the first half of the night.

msg:This mid-mountain trip is a temporary rise.
I accidentally brushed the infusion in the ward. Ctrip recommended it. With the mentality of giving it a try, I clicked on the reservation. Fortunately, there was a room.
In fact, the expectations for this kind of Internet celebrity shop are not high. Jiaoding Mountain and Niubei Mountain, the Internet celebrity check-in time and time again, has seen too many cases, beautiful scenery, and unsuitable supporting cases. But the mid-levels are really pleasant surprises. Whether it's eating, playing, everything is available, and for a tent hotel, it's really clean. The food is also super delicious and the price is reasonable. The waiters are also very friendly. The only downside is that you need to go up the mountain by yourself, which is equivalent to climbing the mountain before staying in the hotel. It is a bit specific for an elderly person like me. Second, the sheets are relatively damp in the mountains, but they are equipped with electric blankets and heaters, which have little impact and no mildew. taste. This time it is an early exploration, and I will come again when the children are on vacation in the middle of the mountain. The first choice for couples and parents and children. ps, for this kind of place, it is still relatively weather-beating. Check the weather forecast in advance when you go out. The sun is definitely worth the fare, awesome
